             The operating rules of the refinery.
             The physics of this particular factory.
             Each principle feels like "a law of physics being named ‚Äî
             not invented, recognized."
             R3: density MEDIUM ‚Äî conceptual weight high, spatial moderate
             R5: alternating velocity ‚Äî quote (slow) + explanation (medium)
             ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê -->
        <section id="core-principles" class="section" aria-label="Core Principles">
          <div class="section-meta">Principles Stratum ¬∑ Operating Rules</div>
          <h2>Core Principles</h2>


          <!-- ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
               GUPP: The Universal Propulsion Principle
               The MOST important principle ‚Äî gets full structural treatment.
               2-zone block (header/body) with red border-left.
               R5: first component sets section tone ‚Äî GUPP sets authority.
               Mechanism #10: Red border-left = highest semantic weight
               Mechanism #2: 2-zone structure for gravity
               ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ -->
          <div class="gupp-block">
            <div class="gupp-header">
              <h3>GUPP: The Universal Propulsion Principle</h3>
            </div>
            <div class="gupp-body">

              <blockquote class="key-quote">
                <p>"If there is work on your hook, YOU MUST RUN IT."</p>
              </blockquote>

              <p>This solves the fundamental problem that "Claude Code ends":</p>

              <ul>
                <li>Work is "slung" to agent hooks (persistent git worktrees)</li>
                <li>When an agent starts, it checks its hook</li>
                <li>If work exists, execution is immediate ‚Äî no confirmation, no waiting</li>
                <li>Work survives crashes and restarts</li>
              </ul>

              <p><strong>The Gupp Nudge:</strong> Claude Code is "so miserably polite" that GUPP doesn't always work. Gas Town implements a "Gupp Nudge" ‚Äî agents get a startup poke with <code>gt nudge</code> roughly 30-60 seconds after starting.</p>
            </div>
          </div>


          <!-- R5: spacing shift between principles (same domain, same intensity) -->
          <hr class="section-divider" aria-hidden="true">


          <!-- ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
               Zero Framework Cognition
               R5: essence callout ‚Üí quote (slow) + explanation (medium)
               R5: S5 teaching moment ‚Üí principle ‚Üí practical
               ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ -->
          <div class="principle-block">
            <h3>Zero Framework Cognition</h3>

            <blockquote class="key-quote">
              <p>"Claude makes all decisions. The orchestrator executes."</p>
            </blockquote>

            <p><strong>Key design principle:</strong> All decisions delegated to AI. No heuristics, regex, or parsing in the orchestrator. The framework provides infrastructure, not intelligence.</p>
          </div>


          <!-- ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
               Agents as Cattle, Not Pets
               Kubernetes thinking applied to agents.
               R5: temperature = NEUTRAL (systematic, structural)
               ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ -->
          <div class="principle-block">
            <h3>Agents as Cattle, Not Pets</h3>

            <p>This is Kubernetes thinking applied to agents:</p>

            <ul class="cattle-list">
              <li>Individual sessions are <strong>ephemeral</strong></li>
              <li>The work graph is <strong>persistent</strong></li>
              <li>The agent is not the session</li>
              <li>The agent is a Bead (identity with a global address)</li>
            </ul>
          </div>


          <!-- ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
               Nondeterministic Idempotence
               R5: temperature = WARM (amber) ‚Äî resilience, not alarm
               ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ -->
          <div class="principle-block">
            <h3>Nondeterministic Idempotence</h3>

            <p>Workflows can be interrupted and resumed at any time:</p>

            <ul class="idem-list">
              <li>Path is fully nondeterministic ‚Äî different runs take different routes</li>
              <li>Workflow eventually finishes as long as you keep throwing agents at it</li>
              <li>Agents may make mistakes but self-correct because acceptance criteria are well-specified</li>
              <li>The system is resilient to individual component failures</li>
            </ul>
          </div>


          <!-- ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
               Token Spend as Health Metric
               R5: data-heavy principle ‚Äî quote + math
               Mechanism #18: structured data (the math block)
               ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ -->
          <div class="principle-block">
            <h3>Token Spend as Health Metric</h3>

            <blockquote class="key-quote">
              <p>"Token spend per developer per unit time is the new health metric that best represents how well your company is doing with AI."</p>
            </blockquote>

            <div class="token-math">
              <strong>Agent cost:</strong> ~$10-12 per operating hour<br>
              <strong>Recommended daily budget:</strong> $100-300<br>
              <strong>Yegge's personal spend:</strong> ~$300/day, ~$80,000/year<br>
              <strong>Output:</strong> Gas Town workshops generate 12,000 LOC/day per developer
            </div>
          </div>


          <!-- ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
               Talk to the Plan, Not the Agent
               R5: S4 resolution ‚Äî closing principle, practical wisdom
               R5: temperature = WARM ‚Üí grounding, not abstract
               ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ -->
          <div class="principle-block">
            <h3>Talk to the Plan, Not the Agent</h3>

            <p>Because agents have limited context windows and experience "amnesia":</p>

            <ul class="plan-list">
              <li>Maintain persistent, readable <strong>plans in files</strong></li>
              <li>Both you and agents <strong>reference these plans</strong></li>
              <li><strong>"Land the Plane" pattern:</strong> At session end, clean up git, update issues, spit out prompt for next session</li>
            </ul>
          </div>


          <!-- R5: challenge callout ‚Äî section closer for principles
               Invitation to synthesize. Warm, not demanding.
               R5: S4 resolution ‚Äî end with invitation, not anxiety -->
          <div class="callout callout--challenge" role="note">
            <div class="callout-label">Challenge</div>
            <div class="callout-body">
              <p>Which of these six principles already describes something you do intuitively? Which feels alien? The ones that feel alien are where Gas Town will change how you think about agent orchestration ‚Äî not just what tools you use, but what you believe about how software gets built.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

        </section>


      </div>
    </div>


    <!-- ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê
         SURFACE STRATUM ‚Äî Implementation
         Where the reader's hands meet the machine.
         Relief. Grounding. go install, gt init, tmux layouts.
         Arc: After conceptual density, concrete surfaces. "I could actually do this."
         Density: MEDIUM ‚Üí practical, structured, breathing.
         Transition: HARD CUT from Principles (domain change: concepts ‚Üí practice)
         R3: density transition from conceptual HIGH to practical MEDIUM
         ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê -->

          <h2>Implementation Guide</h2>


          <!-- ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê
               Prerequisites Checklist
               Reuses the bouncer-checklist pattern from Foundation.
               Red accent recurs ‚Äî this time for practical gate-keeping.
               R5: S3 first component = checklist ‚Üí sets practical tone
               ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê -->
          <h3>Prerequisites Checklist</h3>

          <p>Before installing Gas Town, verify:</p>

          <div class="prerequisites">
            <div class="prerequisites-label">Required</div>
            <ul class="prerequisites-list">
              <li><span class="check-marker"></span><strong>Go 1.21+</strong> installed (<code>go version</code>)</li>
              <li><span class="check-marker"></span><strong>tmux</strong> installed and proficient (<code>tmux -V</code>)</li>
              <li><span class="check-marker"></span><strong>Multiple Claude accounts</strong> for parallel agents</li>
              <li><span class="check-marker"></span><strong>Stage 7+ experience</strong> (100+ hours multi-agent)</li>
              <li><span class="check-marker"></span><strong>High chaos tolerance</strong> (some bugs, some lost work)</li>
              <li><span class="check-marker"></span><strong>Budget:</strong> $50-200/day</li>
            </ul>
          </div>


          <!-- R5: spacing shift ‚Äî prerequisites ‚Üí installation -->
          <hr class="section-divider" aria-hidden="true">


          <!-- ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê
               Installation
               Step-by-step with checkpoint verification markers.
               Mechanism #17: Code blocks for CLI commands
               Mechanism #12: Progressive disclosure (step sequence)
               ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê -->
          <h3>Installation</h3>

          <div class="install-step">
            <div class="code-block"><code><span class="cmt"># Step 1: Install Gas Town</span>
<span class="fn">go</span> <span class="str">install</span> github.com/steveyegge/gastown/cmd/gt@latest

<span class="cmt"># Step 2: Verify installation</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">version</span>

<span class="cmt"># Step 3: Initialize your town (creates ~/.gt)</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">init</span></code></div>

            <div class="checkpoint-marker">Checkpoint: You should see "Town initialized at ~/.gt"</div>
          </div>


          <!-- R5: spacing shift ‚Äî install ‚Üí first rig -->
          <hr class="section-divider" aria-hidden="true">


          <!-- ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê
               Adding Your First Rig
               ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê -->
          <h3>Adding Your First Rig</h3>

          <div class="install-step">
            <div class="code-block"><code><span class="cmt"># Add a project rig</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">rig</span> <span class="str">add</span> /path/to/your/project

<span class="cmt"># Verify</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">rig</span> <span class="str">list</span></code></div>

            <div class="checkpoint-marker">Checkpoint: Your project should appear in the rig list</div>
          </div>


          <!-- R5: spacing shift ‚Äî first rig ‚Üí starting roles -->
          <hr class="section-divider" aria-hidden="true">


          <!-- ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê
               Starting the Core Roles
               The startup sequence mirrors the role hierarchy:
               town-level first, then rig-level, then workers.
               R5: code snippet velocity = SLOW ‚Üí needs breathing room
               ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê -->
          <h3>Starting the Core Roles</h3>

          <p>Recommended startup sequence:</p>

          <div class="startup-sequence">
            <div class="startup-phase">
              <div class="startup-phase-label">1. Town-level roles first</div>
              <div class="code-block"><code><span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">mayor</span> <span class="str">up</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">deacon</span> <span class="str">up</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">dogs</span> <span class="str">up</span></code></div>
            </div>

            <div class="startup-phase">
              <div class="startup-phase-label">2. Rig-level infrastructure</div>
              <div class="code-block"><code><span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">witness</span> <span class="str">up</span> my-project
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">refinery</span> <span class="str">up</span> my-project</code></div>
            </div>

            <div class="startup-phase">
              <div class="startup-phase-label">3. Named workers</div>
              <div class="code-block"><code><span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">polecat</span> <span class="str">up</span> my-project alice
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">polecat</span> <span class="str">up</span> my-project bob
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">polecat</span> <span class="str">up</span> my-project carol</code></div>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div class="checkpoint-marker">Checkpoint: <code>gt status</code> should show all roles running</div>


          <!-- R5: spacing shift ‚Äî roles ‚Üí tmux -->
          <hr class="section-divider" aria-hidden="true">


          <!-- ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê
               tmux Workflow
               Gas Town is tmux-native. This diagram shows the workspace.
               Mechanism #15: Bento grid for spatial mapping
               Mechanism #13: Dark title bar echoes refinery header
               R4: hub-and-spoke ‚Äî overview is the hub
               ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê -->
          <h3>tmux Workflow</h3>

          <p>Gas Town is tmux-native. Understand this structure:</p>

          <div class="tmux-diagram" role="figure" aria-label="tmux session layout showing Gas Town windows: mayor, polecats, and overview monitor">
            <div class="tmux-title">tmux session: gastown</div>
            <div class="tmux-grid">
              <div class="tmux-window">
                <div class="tmux-window-name">mayor</div>
                <div class="tmux-window-role">Mayor Agent</div>
              </div>
              <div class="tmux-window">
                <div class="tmux-window-name">alice</div>
                <div class="tmux-window-role">Polecat Alice</div>
              </div>
              <div class="tmux-window">
                <div class="tmux-window-name">bob</div>
                <div class="tmux-window-role">Polecat Bob</div>
              </div>
              <div class="tmux-window tmux-window--overview">
                <div class="tmux-window-name">overview</div>
                <div class="tmux-window-role">rpai ‚Äî Agent Status Monitor</div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>


          <!-- R5: spacing shift ‚Äî tmux ‚Üí startup script -->
          <hr class="section-divider" aria-hidden="true">


          <!-- ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê
               Startup Script
               The longest code block on the page ‚Äî the section's density peak.
               R5: code wall anti-pattern awareness ‚Äî but this IS a reference script,
               so the full block is appropriate. Preceded by context, followed by breathing.
               Mechanism #17: Code block at maximum density
               ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê -->
          <h3>Startup Script</h3>

          <!-- R5: info callout ‚Äî context BEFORE the code wall
               R5: S6 anti-pattern A6 prevention ‚Äî never orphan code without context -->
          <div class="callout callout--info" role="note">
            <div class="callout-label">Reference Script</div>
            <div class="callout-body">
              <p>Save this as <code>gastown-start.sh</code>. This creates a full tmux session with all roles, rig windows, and polecat workspaces. Run with <code>--fresh</code> to kill any existing session first.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div class="code-block"><code><span class="cmt">#!/bin/bash</span>
<span class="typ">SESSION</span><span class="pn">=</span><span class="str">"gastown"</span>

<span class="cmt"># Kill existing session if requested</span>
<span class="kw">if</span> <span class="pn">[</span> <span class="str">"$1"</span> <span class="pn">=</span> <span class="str">"--fresh"</span> <span class="pn">];</span> <span class="kw">then</span>
  <span class="fn">tmux</span> kill-session -t <span class="typ">$SESSION</span> <span class="num">2</span>&gt;/dev/null
<span class="kw">fi</span>

<span class="cmt"># Create session</span>
<span class="fn">tmux</span> new-session -d -s <span class="typ">$SESSION</span> -n <span class="str">'overview'</span>

<span class="cmt"># Infrastructure windows</span>
<span class="fn">tmux</span> new-window -t <span class="typ">$SESSION</span> -n <span class="str">'mayor'</span>
<span class="fn">tmux</span> new-window -t <span class="typ">$SESSION</span> -n <span class="str">'infra'</span>
<span class="fn">tmux</span> split-window -h -t <span class="typ">$SESSION</span>:infra

<span class="cmt"># Per-rig windows</span>
<span class="kw">for</span> <span class="typ">RIG</span> <span class="kw">in</span> project1 project2<span class="pn">;</span> <span class="kw">do</span>
  <span class="fn">tmux</span> new-window -t <span class="typ">$SESSION</span> -n <span class="str">"rig-$RIG"</span>
  <span class="fn">tmux</span> split-window -h -t <span class="str">"rig-$RIG"</span>
<span class="kw">done</span>

<span class="cmt"># Polecat windows</span>
<span class="kw">for</span> <span class="typ">POLECAT</span> <span class="kw">in</span> alice bob carol<span class="pn">;</span> <span class="kw">do</span>
  <span class="fn">tmux</span> new-window -t <span class="typ">$SESSION</span> -n <span class="str">"$POLECAT"</span>
<span class="kw">done</span>

<span class="cmt"># Inbox window</span>
<span class="fn">tmux</span> new-window -t <span class="typ">$SESSION</span> -n <span class="str">'inbox'</span>

<span class="cmt"># Start roles</span>
<span class="fn">tmux</span> send-keys -t <span class="typ">$SESSION</span>:mayor <span class="str">'gt mayor up'</span> C-m
<span class="fn">tmux</span> send-keys -t <span class="typ">$SESSION</span>:infra.0 <span class="str">'gt deacon up'</span> C-m
<span class="fn">tmux</span> send-keys -t <span class="typ">$SESSION</span>:infra.1 <span class="str">'gt dogs up'</span> C-m
<span class="fn">tmux</span> send-keys -t <span class="typ">$SESSION</span>:rig-project1.0 <span class="str">'gt witness up project1'</span> C-m
<span class="fn">tmux</span> send-keys -t <span class="typ">$SESSION</span>:rig-project1.1 <span class="str">'gt refinery up project1'</span> C-m
<span class="fn">tmux</span> send-keys -t <span class="typ">$SESSION</span>:alice <span class="str">'gt polecat up project1 alice'</span> C-m
<span class="fn">tmux</span> send-keys -t <span class="typ">$SESSION</span>:bob <span class="str">'gt polecat up project1 bob'</span> C-m
<span class="fn">tmux</span> send-keys -t <span class="typ">$SESSION</span>:inbox <span class="str">'watch -n 5 gt inbox'</span> C-m

<span class="cmt"># Attach</span>
<span class="fn">tmux</span> select-window -t <span class="typ">$SESSION</span>:overview
<span class="fn">tmux</span> attach -t <span class="typ">$SESSION</span></code></div>


          <!-- R5: spacing shift ‚Äî startup script ‚Üí daily workflow -->
          <hr class="section-divider" aria-hidden="true">


          <!-- ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê
               Typical Daily Workflow
               The reader watches someone's morning routine.
               Intimate, practical, demystifying.
               R3: temporal density ‚Äî information unfolds over daily cycle
               R5: annotated code = SLOW velocity + practical temperature
               ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê -->
          <h3>Typical Daily Workflow</h3>

          <div class="workflow-block">

            <div class="workflow-phase">
              <div class="workflow-phase-label">Morning: Start Town</div>
              <div class="code-block"><code><span class="cmt"># Morning: Start town</span>
./gastown-start.sh

<span class="cmt"># Review overnight status</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">status</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">inbox</span></code></div>
            </div>

            <div class="workflow-phase">
              <div class="workflow-phase-label">Midday: File and Monitor</div>
              <div class="code-block"><code><span class="cmt"># File new feature</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">inbox</span> <span class="str">send</span> my-project <span class="str">"Build user authentication"</span>

<span class="cmt"># Refinery decomposes, assigns to polecats</span>
<span class="cmt"># You review pending decisions</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">inbox</span> <span class="str">respond</span> <span class="num">5</span> --approve
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">inbox</span> <span class="str">respond</span> <span class="num">7</span> --approve

<span class="cmt"># Monitor throughout day (switch tmux windows)</span>
<span class="cmt"># Dogs run quality checks automatically</span></code></div>
            </div>

            <div class="workflow-phase">
              <div class="workflow-phase-label">Evening: Review and Close</div>
              <div class="code-block"><code><span class="cmt"># Evening: Review completed work</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">inbox</span> <span class="str">review</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">approve</span> <span class="num">12</span> <span class="num">15</span> <span class="num">18</span>  <span class="cmt"># Approve completed items</span>

<span class="cmt"># End of day (polecats persist, crew killed)</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">crew</span> <span class="str">purge</span> my-project</code></div>
            </div>

          </div>

          <!-- R5: tip callout ‚Äî warm, grounding, section closure
               The daily workflow is intimate ‚Äî the tip makes it personal
               R5: S4 resolution ‚Üí end on practical warmth -->
          <div class="callout callout--tip" role="note">
            <div class="callout-label">Tip</div>
            <div class="callout-body">
              <p>Polecats persist across sessions ‚Äî they have identity and memory through Beads. Crew members are ephemeral. At end of day, purge the crew but leave your polecats running. They'll pick up where they left off tomorrow, guided by GUPP.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <!-- R5: gotcha callout ‚Äî protective warning near section end
               The chaos-management truth: things WILL go wrong
               R5: gotcha temperature = COLD but followed by tip = arc -->
          <div class="callout callout--gotcha" role="note">
            <div class="callout-label">Gotcha</div>
            <div class="callout-body">
              <p>The startup script assumes a single rig. If you're running multiple projects, duplicate the per-rig and polecat sections. And yes ‚Äî "some bugs fixed 2-3 times" and "some fixes get lost" is the reality. Nondeterministic idempotence means the work gets done; it doesn't mean the path is clean.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

        </section>


      </div>
    </div>


    <!-- ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê
         SURFACE STRATUM CONTINUED ‚Äî Checkpoints + Troubleshooting
         Still the surface level where hands meet the machine.
         Verificatory ‚Üí Diagnostic: "verify you did it right" then "when it breaks"
         R3: density MEDIUM-LOW, structured, practical
         R5: S4 resolution ‚Üí verification resolves installation, troubleshooting resolves failures
         ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê -->
    <div class="stratum stratum--surface">
      <div class="page-spine">


        <!-- ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê
             SECTION 9: CHECKPOINTS AND VERIFICATION
             Verificatory territory. The instrument panel.
             After "do this," this section says "verify you did it right."
             Density: LOW-MEDIUM ‚Äî tables and code, minimal prose
             R5: S1 setup-payoff ‚Üí Demo (table) + Action (code commands)
             ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê -->
        <section id="checkpoints-and-verification" class="section" aria-label="Checkpoints and Verification">
          <div class="section-meta">Surface Stratum ¬∑ Verification</div>
          <h2>8. Checkpoints and Verification</h2>

          <h3>Post-Installation Checkpoints</h3>

          <!-- Mechanism #18: Data Table ‚Äî verification steps as instrument readings
               R5: table format serves binary verification: command ‚Üí expected output -->
          <table class="data-table">
            <thead>
              <tr>
                <th>Step</th>
                <th>Command</th>
                <th>Expected Output</th>
              </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>
              <tr>
                <td><strong>Go installed</strong></td>
                <td><code>go version</code></td>
                <td><code>go version go1.21+</code></td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><strong>gt installed</strong></td>
                <td><code>gt version</code></td>
                <td>Version number</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><strong>Town initialized</strong></td>
                <td><code>gt status</code></td>
                <td>Shows town state</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><strong>Rig added</strong></td>
                <td><code>gt rig list</code></td>
                <td>Shows your project</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><strong>Mayor running</strong></td>
                <td><code>gt mayor status</code></td>
                <td><code>running</code></td>
              </tr>
            </tbody>
          </table>

          <h3>Health Checks</h3>

          <!-- Mechanism #17: Code Block ‚Äî dark background, diagnostic commands -->
          <div class="code-block"><code><span class="cmt"># Check all role status</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">status</span>

<span class="cmt"># Check specific rig</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">rig</span> <span class="str">status</span> my-project

<span class="cmt"># View agent health</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">deacon</span> <span class="str">report</span></code></div>

          <p><strong>Healthy state indicators:</strong></p>

          <!-- Green-accented health list ‚Äî Mechanism #9: green = healthy
               R5: resolution list after diagnostic code -->
          <ul class="health-indicators">
            <li>All roles show <code>running</code></li>
            <li>Deacon reports no anomalies</li>
            <li>Inbox has reasonable pending items (not 100+)</li>
            <li>Polecats are progressing on tasks</li>
          </ul>

          <h3>Quality Verification</h3>

          <div class="code-block"><code><span class="cmt"># Trigger Dogs quality check</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">dogs</span> <span class="str">bark</span>

<span class="cmt"># Review what passed/failed</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">dogs</span> <span class="str">report</span></code></div>

        </section>


        <!-- Spacing shift transition within surface stratum
             Type 2: same domain, different intensity (verification ‚Üí diagnostic)
             R5: section boundary = 1px separator -->
        <hr class="section-divider" aria-hidden="true">


        <!-- ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê
             SECTION 10: TROUBLESHOOTING
             Diagnostic territory. When it breaks.
             Structured repeating pattern: Symptom ‚Üí Cause ‚Üí Recovery
             Density: MEDIUM ‚Äî 6 failure blocks, each self-contained
             Arc: each failure has a clear recovery. Not anxiety ‚Äî competence.
             R5: Troubleshooting Recipe ‚Üí gotcha + code + tip pattern
             ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê -->
        <section id="troubleshooting" class="section" aria-label="Troubleshooting">
          <div class="section-meta">Surface Stratum ¬∑ Diagnostic</div>
          <h2>9. Troubleshooting</h2>

          <h3>Common Failures and Recovery</h3>

          <!-- R5: structured repeating pattern ‚Äî each failure block is a self-contained
               diagnostic unit. The repetition creates rhythm without monotony because
               each recovery is different (reset, worktrees, kill, approve, sync, config).
               Mechanism #2: 2-zone header/body on each failure block -->

          <!-- Failure 1: Context Collapse -->
          <div class="failure-block">
            <div class="failure-header">
              <span class="failure-number">01</span>
              <span class="failure-name">Context Collapse</span>
            </div>
            <div class="failure-body">
              <div class="failure-field">
                <div class="failure-field-label">Symptom</div>
                <p>Agents stop making sense, circular reasoning</p>
              </div>
              <div class="failure-field">
                <div class="failure-field-label">Cause</div>
                <p>Beads state corruption or no auto-compact</p>
              </div>
              <div class="failure-field">
                <div class="failure-field-label">Recovery</div>
                <div class="code-block" style="margin: var(--space-3) 0 0 0;"><code><span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">town</span> <span class="str">reset</span> <span class="num">--soft</span>   <span class="cmt"># Keep config, clear state</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">beads</span> <span class="str">sync</span> <span class="num">--force</span>  <span class="cmt"># Force context resync</span></code></div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

          <!-- Failure 2: Race Conditions -->
          <div class="failure-block">
            <div class="failure-header">
              <span class="failure-number">02</span>
              <span class="failure-name">Race Conditions / Merge Conflicts</span>
            </div>
            <div class="failure-body">
              <div class="failure-field">
                <div class="failure-field-label">Symptom</div>
                <p>Conflicting commits, overwritten work</p>
              </div>
              <div class="failure-field">
                <div class="failure-field-label">Cause</div>
                <p>Multiple Polecats editing same files</p>
              </div>
              <div class="failure-field">
                <div class="failure-field-label">Recovery</div>
                <p>Use git worktrees for file isolation. Implement file ownership rules. Use the Refinery's merge queue.</p>
                <div class="code-block" style="margin: var(--space-3) 0 0 0;"><code><span class="cmt"># Check for conflicts</span>
<span class="fn">git</span> <span class="str">status</span>

<span class="cmt"># If conflicts exist</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">refinery</span> <span class="str">resolve</span> my-project</code></div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

          <!-- Failure 3: Runaway Crew -->
          <div class="failure-block">
            <div class="failure-header">
              <span class="failure-number">03</span>
              <span class="failure-name">Runaway Crew</span>
            </div>
            <div class="failure-body">
              <div class="failure-field">
                <div class="failure-field-label">Symptom</div>
                <p>Cost spike, dozens of Crew spawned unexpectedly</p>
              </div>
              <div class="failure-field">
                <div class="failure-field-label">Cause</div>
                <p>Refinery misconfiguration or task explosion</p>
              </div>
              <div class="failure-field">
                <div class="failure-field-label">Recovery</div>
                <div class="code-block" style="margin: var(--space-3) 0 0 0;"><code><span class="cmt"># Kill all crew immediately</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">crew</span> <span class="str">purge</span> <span class="num">--all</span>

<span class="cmt"># Set limits</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">config</span> <span class="str">set</span> crew.max_per_rig <span class="num">5</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">config</span> <span class="str">set</span> crew.idle_timeout <span class="num">15</span></code></div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

          <!-- Failure 4: Mayor Deadlock -->
          <div class="failure-block">
            <div class="failure-header">
              <span class="failure-number">04</span>
              <span class="failure-name">Mayor Deadlock</span>
            </div>
            <div class="failure-body">
              <div class="failure-field">
                <div class="failure-field-label">Symptom</div>
                <p>No work getting assigned, town seems stuck</p>
              </div>
              <div class="failure-field">
                <div class="failure-field-label">Cause</div>
                <p>Mayor waiting for human decision on something</p>
              </div>
              <div class="failure-field">
                <div class="failure-field-label">Recovery</div>
                <div class="code-block" style="margin: var(--space-3) 0 0 0;"><code><span class="cmt"># Check inbox</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">inbox</span>

<span class="cmt"># Approve/reject pending items</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">inbox</span> <span class="str">respond</span> &lt;id&gt; <span class="num">--approve</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">inbox</span> <span class="str">respond</span> &lt;id&gt; <span class="num">--reject</span></code></div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

          <!-- Failure 5: Beads Desync -->
          <div class="failure-block">
            <div class="failure-header">
              <span class="failure-number">05</span>
              <span class="failure-name">Beads Desync</span>
            </div>
            <div class="failure-body">
              <div class="failure-field">
                <div class="failure-field-label">Symptom</div>
                <p>Agents have stale context, working on old state</p>
              </div>
              <div class="failure-field">
                <div class="failure-field-label">Cause</div>
                <p>Git conflicts in Beads repo</p>
              </div>
              <div class="failure-field">
                <div class="failure-field-label">Recovery</div>
                <div class="code-block" style="margin: var(--space-3) 0 0 0;"><code><span class="cmt"># Force sync</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">beads</span> <span class="str">sync</span> <span class="num">--force</span>

<span class="cmt"># If that fails, reset Beads</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">beads</span> <span class="str">reset</span></code></div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

          <!-- Failure 6: Agent Won't Start -->
          <div class="failure-block">
            <div class="failure-header">
              <span class="failure-number">06</span>
              <span class="failure-name">Agent Won't Start</span>
            </div>
            <div class="failure-body">
              <div class="failure-field">
                <div class="failure-field-label">Symptom</div>
                <p><code>gt polecat up</code> returns error</p>
              </div>
              <div class="failure-field">
                <div class="failure-field-label">Cause</div>
                <p>Claude account issue, rate limiting, or config problem</p>
              </div>
              <div class="failure-field">
                <div class="failure-field-label">Recovery</div>
                <div class="code-block" style="margin: var(--space-3) 0 0 0;"><code><span class="cmt"># Check config</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">config</span> <span class="str">list</span>

<span class="cmt"># Try different account</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">config</span> <span class="str">set</span> polecat.alice.account secondary

<span class="cmt"># Check Claude status</span>
<span class="fn">claude</span> <span class="num">--version</span></code></div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>


          <!-- Recovery Command Reference ‚Äî the emergency procedures card
               Dense, comprehensive, dark-header format like the hierarchy diagram.
               Everything you need to recover, in one place.
               Mechanism #13: dark title bar signals authority
               R5: S4 resolution ‚Üí comprehensive ending resolves section tension -->
          <h3>Recovery Command Reference</h3>

          <div class="recovery-ref">
            <div class="recovery-ref-title">Emergency Recovery Commands</div>
            <div class="code-block" style="margin: 0; border-top: none;"><code><span class="cmt"># Soft reset (keep config)</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">town</span> <span class="str">reset</span> <span class="num">--soft</span>

<span class="cmt"># Hard reset (full reinstall)</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">town</span> <span class="str">reset</span> <span class="num">--hard</span>

<span class="cmt"># Kill all agents</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">town</span> <span class="str">down</span>

<span class="cmt"># Restart specific role</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">polecat</span> <span class="str">down</span> my-project alice
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">polecat</span> <span class="str">up</span> my-project alice

<span class="cmt"># Force Beads sync</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">beads</span> <span class="str">sync</span> <span class="num">--force</span>

<span class="cmt"># Clear inbox backlog</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">inbox</span> <span class="str">clear</span> <span class="num">--all</span>

<span class="cmt"># Emergency cost stop</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">pause</span> <span class="num">--all</span>  <span class="cmt"># Pause all work</span>
<span class="fn">gt</span> <span class="str">resume</span> <span class="num">--all</span> <span class="cmt"># Resume when ready</span></code></div>
          </div>

          <!-- R5: tip callout ‚Äî warm resolution after diagnostic density
               Prevents anxiety ending (anti-pattern A7) -->
          <div class="callout callout--tip" role="note">
            <div class="callout-label">Tip</div>
            <div class="callout-body">
              <p>When in doubt, <code>gt pause --all</code> stops all work immediately without losing state. The most expensive mistake is letting runaway agents burn tokens while you diagnose the problem. Pause first, investigate second.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

        </section>


      </div>
    </div>


    <!-- ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê
         HARD CUT: Surface ‚Üí Dispatch
         Domain change: from "doing" to "deciding."
         The 3px red border signals the reader has left operational territory
         and entered evaluation territory. The loading dock.
         Transition Grammar Type 1: HARD CUT (different domains)
         ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê -->


    <!-- ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê

             SECTION 11: WHEN TO USE GAS TOWN
             Evaluative. The master craftsman saying "this tool isn't for every job."
             Generous, not defensive.
             Density: MEDIUM ‚Äî lists + decision flowchart
             Arc: use/don't-use ‚Üí decision tree ‚Üí reader leaves oriented

        <section id="when-to-use-gas-town" class="section" aria-label="When to Use Gas Town">
          <div class="section-meta">Dispatch Stratum ¬∑ Evaluation</div>
          <h2>10. When to Use Gas Town</h2>

          <!-- Use/Don't Use ‚Äî two-column comparison
               Green for use, coral for don't.
               Generous honesty: the "don't" column is as detailed as the "do."
               Mechanism #9: Color encoding (green/coral)
               R5: complementary pairing ‚Äî use + don't creates balanced evaluation -->
          <div class="use-comparison">
            <div class="use-block use-block--yes">
              <h3>Use Gas Town When:</h3>
              <ul>
                <li>You're at Stage 7+ (10+ agents, comfortable with chaos)</li>
                <li>Budget is not a concern ($50-200/day)</li>
                <li>You want <strong>team-scale output</strong> as a solo developer</li>
                <li>You have clear product vision but need implementation velocity</li>
                <li>You're comfortable with imperfection (some bugs fixed 2-3 times)</li>
                <li>You have tmux proficiency</li>
                <li>You understand the PM ‚Üí engineering team mental model</li>
              </ul>
            </div>
            <div class="use-block use-block--no">
              <h3>Don't Use Gas Town When:</h3>
              <ul>
                <li>You're below Stage 6 on the dev evolution scale</li>
                <li>Budget is constrained</li>
                <li>You need polish and stability</li>
                <li>You need predictable, controlled outcomes</li>
                <li>You're not comfortable with chaos</li>
                <li>The project is simple enough for Ralph loops</li>
                <li>You haven't mastered Levels 0-6 on the complexity ladder</li>
              </ul>
            </div>
          </div>

          <h3>Decision Matrix</h3>

          <!-- Decision flowchart ‚Äî vertical, decisive
               Adapted from complexity ladder pattern.
               Each question narrows the decision space.
               Terminal node uses 4px red border ‚Äî the ALARM moment:
               Gas Town is the answer only if you pass every gate.
               Mechanism #1: Border-weight gradient ‚Üí 4px on terminal
               R4: progressive disclosure ‚Äî each question reveals more specificity -->
          <div class="decision-flow" role="figure" aria-label="Decision flowchart for choosing an orchestrator">
            <div class="decision-flow-title">Which Orchestrator?</div>

            <div class="decision-node decision-node--question">Are you Stage 7+?</div>
            <div class="decision-node decision-node--redirect"><span class="decision-label decision-label--no">No ‚Üí</span> Use Ralph Wiggum or CC Mirror</div>
            <div class="decision-connector"></div>

            <div class="decision-node decision-node--question"><span class="decision-label decision-label--yes">Yes ‚Üì</span> Is cost a concern?</div>
            <div class="decision-node decision-node--redirect"><span class="decision-label decision-label--no">Yes ‚Üí</span> Use CC Mirror + Parallel Ralph</div>
            <div class="decision-connector"></div>

            <div class="decision-node decision-node--question"><span class="decision-label decision-label--yes">No ‚Üì</span> Need 24/7 autonomous?</div>
            <div class="decision-node decision-node--redirect"><span class="decision-label decision-label--no">Yes ‚Üí</span> Consider Infinite Orchestra</div>
            <div class="decision-connector"></div>

            <div class="decision-node decision-node--question"><span class="decision-label decision-label--yes">No ‚Üì</span> Want maximum throughput + control?</div>
            <div class="decision-connector"></div>

            <div class="decision-node decision-node--terminal">GAS TOWN</div>
          </div>

          <!-- R5: essence callout ‚Äî the evaluative truth
               Arc: the reader should feel ORIENTED, not sold
               R5: S4 resolution ‚Üí Essence as closure for evaluative section -->
          <div class="callout callout--essence" role="note">
            <div class="callout-label">Essence</div>
            <div class="callout-body">
              <p>Gas Town is not the destination for everyone. It is the destination for people who have exhausted every simpler approach and still need more. If you have any doubt whatsoever, then you can't use it.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

        </section>

          <h2>12. Comparison with Other Patterns</h2>


          <!-- Comparison 1: Gas Town vs Ralph Wiggum -->
          <div class="comparison-section">
            <h3>Gas Town vs Ralph Wiggum</h3>

            <!-- Mechanism #18: Data Table ‚Äî structured comparison
                 R5: Decision Matrix component behavior -->
            <table class="data-table">
              <thead>
                <tr>
                  <th>Aspect</th>
                  <th>Ralph Wiggum</th>
                  <th>Gas Town</th>
                </tr>
              </thead>
              <tbody>
                <tr>
                  <td><strong>Model</strong></td>
                  <td>Single agent, retry loop</td>
                  <td>Multi-agent factory</td>
                </tr>
                <tr>
                  <td><strong>Complexity</strong></td>
                  <td>Bash script</td>
                  <td>Full system</td>
                </tr>
                <tr>
                  <td><strong>Persistence</strong></td>
                  <td>Via git/progress.txt</td>
                  <td>Beads data plane</td>
                </tr>
                <tr>
                  <td><strong>Parallelism</strong></td>
                  <td>None (sequential)</td>
                  <td>Native (many agents)</td>
                </tr>
                <tr>
                  <td><strong>Roles</strong></td>
                  <td>None</td>
                  <td>8 specialized roles</td>
                </tr>
                <tr>
                  <td><strong>Setup</strong></td>
                  <td>Minutes</td>
                  <td>Hours/days</td>
                </tr>
                <tr>
                  <td><strong>Cost</strong></td>
                  <td>Single agent</td>
                  <td>Multiple accounts</td>
                </tr>
                <tr>
                  <td><strong>Use Case</strong></td>
                  <td>Well-defined features</td>
                  <td>Complex systems, ongoing dev</td>
                </tr>
              </tbody>
            </table>

            <div class="comparison-verdict">
              <p><strong>When to use Ralph:</strong> Single feature, clear completion criteria, budget-conscious.</p>
              <p><strong>When to use Gas Town:</strong> Building entire products, team-scale output needed.</p>
            </div>
          </div>


          <!-- Comparison 2: Gas Town vs CC Mirror -->
          <div class="comparison-section">
            <h3>Gas Town vs CC Mirror</h3>

            <table class="data-table">
              <thead>
                <tr>
                  <th>Aspect</th>
                  <th>CC Mirror</th>
                  <th>Gas Town</th>
                </tr>

            <!-- nummanali's take ‚Äî a key external voice
                 Quoted with editorial weight to honor the source -->
            <div class="key-quote" style="margin: var(--space-6) 0;">
              <p>"Simplicity covers 80% with zero effort ‚Äî mass-market ease. Gas Town for remaining 20%." ‚Äî nummanali</p>
            </div>

            <div class="comparison-verdict">
              <p><strong>When to use CC Mirror:</strong> Most projects, getting started with multi-agent.</p>
              <p><strong>When to use Gas Town:</strong> Stage 7+ scale, maximum throughput.</p>
            </div>
          </div>


          <!-- Comparison 3: Gas Town vs Infinite Orchestra -->
          <div class="comparison-section">
            <h3>Gas Town vs Infinite Orchestra</h3>

            <table class="data-table">
              <thead>
                <tr>
                  <th>Aspect</th>
                  <th>Orchestra</th>
                  <th>Gas Town</th>
                </tr>
              </thead>
              <tbody>
                <tr>
                  <td><strong>Model</strong></td>
                  <td>Self-improving</td>
                  <td>Production factory</td>
                </tr>
                <tr>
                  <td><strong>Environment</strong></td>
                  <td>Docker container</td>
                  <td>tmux + local</td>
                </tr>
                <tr>
                  <td><strong>Autonomy</strong></td>
                  <td>High (improves itself)</td>
                  <td>Human-directed</td>
                </tr>
                <tr>
                  <td><strong>Parallelism</strong></td>
                  <td>Sequential (for now)</td>
                  <td>Native parallel</td>
                </tr>
                <tr>
                  <td><strong>Roles</strong></td>
                  <td>Profiles (coder, arch)</td>
                  <td>8 fixed roles</td>
                </tr>
                <tr>
                  <td><strong>Persistence</strong></td>
                  <td>Neo4j optional</td>
                  <td>Beads</td>
                </tr>
                <tr>
                  <td><strong>24/7</strong></td>
                  <td>Yes (designed for)</td>
                  <td>Yes (tmux)</td>
                </tr>
              </tbody>
            </table>

            <div class="comparison-verdict">
              <p><strong>When to use Orchestra:</strong> Experimental, self-evolving systems.</p>
              <p><strong>When to use Gas Town:</strong> Production development, human oversight.</p>
            </div>
          </div>


          <!-- Pattern Comparison Summary ‚Äî the orchestrator spectrum

               Gas Town gets the active/highlighted treatment.
               Mechanism #13: Dark title bar
               Mechanism #15: Grid layout for spatial comparison
               R3: density HIGH ‚Üí maximum information per viewport in closing -->
          <h3>Pattern Comparison Summary</h3>

          <div class="spectrum-bar" role="figure" aria-label="Orchestrator spectrum from simple to complex">

          <div class="section-meta">Dispatch Stratum ¬∑ Appendix A</div>
          <h2>Appendix: Quick Reference</h2>

          <div class="ref-grid">

            <!-- Installation Commands -->
            <div class="ref-category">
              <div class="ref-category-label">Installation</div>
              <div class="code-block">
                <code><span class="cmt"># Install</span>
go install github.com/steveyegge/gastown/cmd/gt@latest

<span class="cmt"># Initialize</span>
gt init
gt rig add /path/to/repo</code>
              </div>
            </div>

            <!-- Role Management -->
            <div class="ref-category">
              <div class="ref-category-label">Role Management</div>
              <div class="code-block">
                <code><span class="cmt"># Town-level</span>
gt mayor up|down|status
gt deacon up|down|status
gt dogs up|down|status|bark

<span class="cmt"># Rig-level</span>
gt witness up|down &lt;rig&gt;
gt refinery up|down &lt;rig&gt;
gt polecat up|down|list &lt;rig&gt; [name]
gt crew spawn|count|purge &lt;rig&gt;</code>
              </div>
            </div>

            <!-- Inbox -->
            <div class="ref-category">
              <div class="ref-category-label">Inbox</div>
              <div class="code-block">
                <code>gt inbox                     <span class="cmt"># View pending</span>
gt inbox respond &lt;id&gt; --approve|--reject
gt inbox clear</code>
              </div>
            </div>

            <!-- Town Management -->
            <div class="ref-category">
              <div class="ref-category-label">Town Management</div>
              <div class="code-block">
                <code>gt status                    <span class="cmt"># Town-wide status</span>
gt town down                 <span class="cmt"># Stop all agents</span>
gt town reset --soft|--hard  <span class="cmt"># Reset state</span>
gt config set|get|list       <span class="cmt"># Configuration</span></code>
              </div>
            </div>

            <!-- Beads ‚Äî spans full width for the most important utility set -->
            <div class="ref-category" style="grid-column: 1 / -1;">
              <div class="ref-category-label">Beads</div>
              <div class="code-block">
                <code>gt beads sync --force
gt beads reset
bd ready
bd create "Task title"
bd dep add &lt;child&gt; &lt;parent&gt;</code>
              </div>
            </div>

          </div>
        </section>

        <!-- ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê
             TAGS + DOCUMENT METADATA
             The very last content. Provenance stamp and topic labels.
             Density: SPARSE ‚Äî metadata, not content. The page breathes out.
             R3: density LOW ‚Üí the final exhale before the footer shell closes
             R5: S4 resolution ‚Üí metadata provides structural closure
             Mechanism #14: Footer mirror principle ‚Äî metadata echoes header
             ‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê -->

## YOUR OBSERVATIONS

Write about what you experience. Use this structure, but write in your own voice. Be specific ‚Äî name files, name moments, name CSS decisions. The next builder reads your observations and must know EXACTLY what you mean.

### 1. DEEPLY INTEGRATED

Material from the corpus that has genuinely shaped the artifact. Not surface references ‚Äî structural influence. Where you can FEEL that the builder read the file deeply and it changed how they built.

The 48px test: If you removed all the CSS the builder added and started from scratch, would they NEED to have read these files to build what they built? If the answer is "no, any builder could have done this without reading the corpus," the integration is surface-level.

Name the specific corpus file. Quote or paraphrase the specific passage. Point to the specific CSS decision or HTML structure that shows deep integration.

### 2. SURFACE-LEVEL

Material that appears referenced but not structurally woven in. The builder seems aware of it ‚Äî maybe a mechanism name appears in a class name, maybe a spacing value matches a number from the research. But the reference does not go deeper than acknowledgment.

This is not failure. It is diagnosis ‚Äî the next builder can deepen these connections.

### 3. ABSENT

Material from the corpus that has no visible influence on the artifact. This is not always a problem ‚Äî some corpus material may genuinely not apply to this content. But if the builder received a file about density progression and the page has uniform density throughout, that absence matters.

Distinguish between "absent because irrelevant to this content" and "absent despite being relevant."

### 4. SURPRISED

Unexpected connections or tensions between the corpus material and the artifact. Places where the builder found something in the material that you would not have predicted. Or places where the material suggests a direction the artifact contradicts.

Surprises are the most valuable observation. They indicate either creative breakthrough (good) or creative misreading (correctable).

### 5. WHAT THE NEXT BUILDER SHOULD ATTEND TO

The 2-3 highest-leverage integration opportunities. Frame these as creative invitations, not defect reports.

Good: "The research on component choreography describes how velocity changes create anticipation ‚Äî the artifact's components currently have uniform pacing. What if the callouts in zone 3 tightened their spacing while zone 5 opened up?"

Bad: "Components lack velocity variation."

Each invitation should name the corpus file, the specific concept, and a concrete creative direction the next builder could explore.

---

Do NOT write CSS. Do NOT suggest specific values. Do NOT use CSS terminology. Write about what you EXPERIENCE ‚Äî using words like heavy, breathing, flat, alive, monotonous, surprising, confident, hesitant, warm, sharp, crowded, spacious, earned, forced.

You are a reader, not a programmer. What do you feel?
